[PDF National Population and Housing Census 2011]
Central Bureau of Statistics (CBS) Nepal is pleased to bring out the series of results of the National Population and Housing Census 2011 (NPHC 2011). The final result of this census was disseminated in November 2012.
URL: https://docs.censusnepal.cbs.gov.np/Documents/db182600-8b0c-4888-89d6-a72fd76efc0e__Volume05Part12.pdf

[2011 Nepal census - Wikipedia]
Nepal conducted a widespread national census in 2011 by the Nepal Central Bureau of Statistics. [2] Working in cooperation with the 58 municipalities and the 3,915 Village Development Committees at a district level, they recorded data from all the municipalities and villages of each district. The data included statistics on population size, households, sex and age distribution, place of birth ...
URL: https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/2011_Nepal_census

[Urdu Speakers in Nepal: 2011 Census Data | PDF | Nepal ...]
The major languages of Nepal (percent spoken as native language) according to the 2011 census are Nepali (44.6%), Maithili (11.7%), Bhojpuri (6.0%), Tharu (5.8%),
URL: https://www.scribd.com/document/238334949/Nepal-p22-24

[ACCORDING | English meaning - Cambridge Dictionary]

URL: https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/according

[Nepal Demographics Profile - IndexMundi]

--- [2011 Nepal census - Wikipedia] ---
Nepal conducted a widespread national census in 2011 by the Nepal Central Bureau of Statistics. Working in cooperation with the 58 municipalities and the 3,915 Village Development Committees at a district level, they recorded data from all the municipalities and villages of each district. The data included statistics on population size, households, sex and age distribution, place of birth, residence characteristics, literacy, marital status, religion, language spoken, caste/ethnic group, economically active population, education, number of children, employment status, and occupation.


--- [Urdu Speakers in Nepal: 2011 Census Data | PDF | Nepal ...] ---
Urdu Speakers in Nepal: 2011 Census Data Nepal has a diverse linguistic heritage with Nepali being the most widely spoken language. The majority of Nepalese follow Hinduism, while Buddhism is also prominent. Kathmandu is the largest city and capital. Nepalese culture is rooted in folklore and reflected in housing, clothing, festivals, and cuisine like dal bhat. Sports like association football and cricket are growing in popularity.
